00665 static CYTHON_INLINE PyObject *__Pyx_GetItemInt_Generic(PyObject *o, PyObject* j) {
00666     PyObject *r;
00667     if (!j) return NULL;
00668     r = PyObject_GetItem(o, j);
00669     Py_DECREF(j);
00670     return r;
00671 }
00672 
00673 
00674 #define __Pyx_GetItemInt_List(o, i, size, to_py_func) (((size) <= sizeof(Py_ssize_t)) ? \
00675                                                     __Pyx_GetItemInt_List_Fast(o, i) : \
00676                                                     __Pyx_GetItemInt_Generic(o, to_py_func(i)))
00677 
00678 static CYTHON_INLINE PyObject *__Pyx_GetItemInt_List_Fast(PyObject *o, Py_ssize_t i) {
00679     if (likely(o != Py_None)) {
00680         if (likely((0 <= i) & (i < PyList_GET_SIZE(o)))) {
00681             PyObject *r = PyList_GET_ITEM(o, i);
00682             Py_INCREF(r);
00683             return r;
00684         }
00685         else if ((-PyList_GET_SIZE(o) <= i) & (i < 0)) {
00686             PyObject *r = PyList_GET_ITEM(o, PyList_GET_SIZE(o) + i);
00687             Py_INCREF(r);
00688             return r;
00689         }
00690     }
00691     return __Pyx_GetItemInt_Generic(o, PyInt_FromSsize_t(i));
00692 }
00693 
00694 #define __Pyx_GetItemInt_Tuple(o, i, size, to_py_func) (((size) <= sizeof(Py_ssize_t)) ? \
00695                                                     __Pyx_GetItemInt_Tuple_Fast(o, i) : \
00696                                                     __Pyx_GetItemInt_Generic(o, to_py_func(i)))
00697 
00698 static CYTHON_INLINE PyObject *__Pyx_GetItemInt_Tuple_Fast(PyObject *o, Py_ssize_t i) {
00699     if (likely(o != Py_None)) {
00700         if (likely((0 <= i) & (i < PyTuple_GET_SIZE(o)))) {
00701             PyObject *r = PyTuple_GET_ITEM(o, i);
00702             Py_INCREF(r);
00703             return r;
00704         }
00705         else if ((-PyTuple_GET_SIZE(o) <= i) & (i < 0)) {
00706             PyObject *r = PyTuple_GET_ITEM(o, PyTuple_GET_SIZE(o) + i);
00707             Py_INCREF(r);
00708             return r;
00709         }
00710     }
00711     return __Pyx_GetItemInt_Generic(o, PyInt_FromSsize_t(i));
00712 }
00713 
00714 
00715 #define __Pyx_GetItemInt(o, i, size, to_py_func) (((size) <= sizeof(Py_ssize_t)) ? \
00716                                                     __Pyx_GetItemInt_Fast(o, i) : \
00717                                                     __Pyx_GetItemInt_Generic(o, to_py_func(i)))
00718 
00719 static CYTHON_INLINE PyObject *__Pyx_GetItemInt_Fast(PyObject *o, Py_ssize_t i) {
00720     PyObject *r;
00721     if (PyList_CheckExact(o) && ((0 <= i) & (i < PyList_GET_SIZE(o)))) {
00722         r = PyList_GET_ITEM(o, i);
00723         Py_INCREF(r);
00724     }
00725     else if (PyTuple_CheckExact(o) && ((0 <= i) & (i < PyTuple_GET_SIZE(o)))) {
00726         r = PyTuple_GET_ITEM(o, i);
00727         Py_INCREF(r);
00728     }
00729     else if (Py_TYPE(o)->tp_as_sequence && Py_TYPE(o)->tp_as_sequence->sq_item && (likely(i >= 0))) {
00730         r = PySequence_GetItem(o, i);
00731     }
00732     else {
00733         r = __Pyx_GetItemInt_Generic(o, PyInt_FromSsize_t(i));
00734     }
00735     return r;
00736 }

03958 static PyObject *__Pyx_GetName(PyObject *dict, PyObject *name) {
03959     PyObject *result;
03960     result = PyObject_GetAttr(dict, name);
03961     if (!result) {
03962         if (dict != __pyx_b) {
03963             PyErr_Clear();
03964             result = PyObject_GetAttr(__pyx_b, name);
03965         }
03966         if (!result) {
03967             PyErr_SetObject(PyExc_NameError, name);
03968         }
03969     }
03970     return result;
03971 }

03973 static void __Pyx_RaiseArgtupleInvalid(
03974     const char* func_name,
03975     int exact,
03976     Py_ssize_t num_min,
03977     Py_ssize_t num_max,
03978     Py_ssize_t num_found)
03979 {
03980     Py_ssize_t num_expected;
03981     const char *more_or_less;
03982 
03983     if (num_found < num_min) {
03984         num_expected = num_min;
03985         more_or_less = "at least";
03986     } else {
03987         num_expected = num_max;
03988         more_or_less = "at most";
03989     }
03990     if (exact) {
03991         more_or_less = "exactly";
03992     }
03993     PyErr_Format(PyExc_TypeError,
03994                  "%s() takes %s %"PY_FORMAT_SIZE_T"d positional argument%s (%"PY_FORMAT_SIZE_T"d given)",
03995                  func_name, more_or_less, num_expected,
03996                  (num_expected == 1) ? "" : "s", num_found);
03997 }
03998 
03999 static CYTHON_INLINE int __Pyx_CheckKeywordStrings(
04000     PyObject *kwdict,
04001     const char* function_name,
04002     int kw_allowed)
04003 {
04004     PyObject* key = 0;
04005     Py_ssize_t pos = 0;
04006     while (PyDict_Next(kwdict, &pos, &key, 0)) {
04007         #if PY_MAJOR_VERSION < 3
04008         if (unlikely(!PyString_CheckExact(key)) && unlikely(!PyString_Check(key)))
04009         #else
04010         if (unlikely(!PyUnicode_CheckExact(key)) && unlikely(!PyUnicode_Check(key)))
04011         #endif
04012             goto invalid_keyword_type;
04013     }
04014     if ((!kw_allowed) && unlikely(key))
04015         goto invalid_keyword;
04016     return 1;
04017 invalid_keyword_type:
04018     PyErr_Format(PyExc_TypeError,
04019         "%s() keywords must be strings", function_name);
04020     return 0;
04021 invalid_keyword:
04022     PyErr_Format(PyExc_TypeError,
04023     #if PY_MAJOR_VERSION < 3
04024         "%s() got an unexpected keyword argument '%s'",
04025         function_name, PyString_AsString(key));
04026     #else
04027         "%s() got an unexpected keyword argument '%U'",
04028         function_name, key);
04029     #endif
04030     return 0;
04031 }
04032 
04033 
04034 static void __Pyx_RaiseDoubleKeywordsError(
04035     const char* func_name,
04036     PyObject* kw_name)
04037 {
04038     PyErr_Format(PyExc_TypeError,
04039         #if PY_MAJOR_VERSION >= 3
04040         "%s() got multiple values for keyword argument '%U'", func_name, kw_name);
04041         #else
04042         "%s() got multiple values for keyword argument '%s'", func_name,
04043         PyString_AS_STRING(kw_name));
04044         #endif
04045 }
04046 
04047 static int __Pyx_ParseOptionalKeywords(
04048     PyObject *kwds,
04049     PyObject **argnames[],
04050     PyObject *kwds2,
04051     PyObject *values[],
04052     Py_ssize_t num_pos_args,
04053     const char* function_name)
04054 {
04055     PyObject *key = 0, *value = 0;
04056     Py_ssize_t pos = 0;
04057     PyObject*** name;
04058     PyObject*** first_kw_arg = argnames + num_pos_args;
04059 
04060     while (PyDict_Next(kwds, &pos, &key, &value)) {
04061         name = first_kw_arg;
04062         while (*name && (**name != key)) name++;
04063         if (*name) {
04064             values[name-argnames] = value;
04065         } else {
04066             #if PY_MAJOR_VERSION < 3
04067             if (unlikely(!PyString_CheckExact(key)) && unlikely(!PyString_Check(key))) {
04068             #else
04069             if (unlikely(!PyUnicode_CheckExact(key)) && unlikely(!PyUnicode_Check(key))) {
04070             #endif
04071                 goto invalid_keyword_type;
04072             } else {
04073                 for (name = first_kw_arg; *name; name++) {
04074                     #if PY_MAJOR_VERSION >= 3
04075                     if (PyUnicode_GET_SIZE(**name) == PyUnicode_GET_SIZE(key) &&
04076                         PyUnicode_Compare(**name, key) == 0) break;
04077                     #else
04078                     if (PyString_GET_SIZE(**name) == PyString_GET_SIZE(key) &&
04079                         _PyString_Eq(**name, key)) break;
04080                     #endif
04081                 }
04082                 if (*name) {
04083                     values[name-argnames] = value;
04084                 } else {
04085                     /* unexpected keyword found */
04086                     for (name=argnames; name != first_kw_arg; name++) {
04087                         if (**name == key) goto arg_passed_twice;
04088                         #if PY_MAJOR_VERSION >= 3
04089                         if (PyUnicode_GET_SIZE(**name) == PyUnicode_GET_SIZE(key) &&
04090                             PyUnicode_Compare(**name, key) == 0) goto arg_passed_twice;
04091                         #else
04092                         if (PyString_GET_SIZE(**name) == PyString_GET_SIZE(key) &&
04093                             _PyString_Eq(**name, key)) goto arg_passed_twice;
04094                         #endif
04095                     }
04096                     if (kwds2) {
04097                         if (unlikely(PyDict_SetItem(kwds2, key, value))) goto bad;
04098                     } else {
04099                         goto invalid_keyword;
04100                     }
04101                 }
04102             }
04103         }
04104     }
04105     return 0;
04106 arg_passed_twice:
04107     __Pyx_RaiseDoubleKeywordsError(function_name, **name);
04108     goto bad;
04109 invalid_keyword_type:
04110     PyErr_Format(PyExc_TypeError,
04111         "%s() keywords must be strings", function_name);
04112     goto bad;
04113 invalid_keyword:
04114     PyErr_Format(PyExc_TypeError,
04115     #if PY_MAJOR_VERSION < 3
04116         "%s() got an unexpected keyword argument '%s'",
04117         function_name, PyString_AsString(key));
04118     #else
04119         "%s() got an unexpected keyword argument '%U'",
04120         function_name, key);
04121     #endif
04122 bad:
04123     return -1;
04124 }

04126 static CYTHON_INLINE void __Pyx_ErrRestore(PyObject *type, PyObject *value, PyObject *tb) {
04127     PyObject *tmp_type, *tmp_value, *tmp_tb;
04128     PyThreadState *tstate = PyThreadState_GET();
04129 
04130     tmp_type = tstate->curexc_type;
04131     tmp_value = tstate->curexc_value;
04132     tmp_tb = tstate->curexc_traceback;
04133     tstate->curexc_type = type;
04134     tstate->curexc_value = value;
04135     tstate->curexc_traceback = tb;
04136     Py_XDECREF(tmp_type);
04137     Py_XDECREF(tmp_value);
04138     Py_XDECREF(tmp_tb);
04139 }
04140 
04141 static CYTHON_INLINE void __Pyx_ErrFetch(PyObject **type, PyObject **value, PyObject **tb) {
04142     PyThreadState *tstate = PyThreadState_GET();
04143     *type = tstate->curexc_type;
04144     *value = tstate->curexc_value;
04145     *tb = tstate->curexc_traceback;
04146 
04147     tstate->curexc_type = 0;
04148     tstate->curexc_value = 0;
04149     tstate->curexc_traceback = 0;
04150 }

04152 
04153 #if PY_MAJOR_VERSION < 3
04154 static void __Pyx_Raise(PyObject *type, PyObject *value, PyObject *tb, PyObject *cause) {
04155     /* cause is unused */
04156     Py_XINCREF(type);
04157     Py_XINCREF(value);
04158     Py_XINCREF(tb);
04159     /* First, check the traceback argument, replacing None with NULL. */
04160     if (tb == Py_None) {
04161         Py_DECREF(tb);
04162         tb = 0;
04163     }
04164     else if (tb != NULL && !PyTraceBack_Check(tb)) {
04165         PyErr_SetString(PyExc_TypeError,
04166             "raise: arg 3 must be a traceback or None");
04167         goto raise_error;
04168     }
04169     /* Next, replace a missing value with None */
04170     if (value == NULL) {
04171         value = Py_None;
04172         Py_INCREF(value);
04173     }
04174     #if PY_VERSION_HEX < 0x02050000
04175     if (!PyClass_Check(type))
04176     #else
04177     if (!PyType_Check(type))
04178     #endif
04179     {
04180         /* Raising an instance.  The value should be a dummy. */
04181         if (value != Py_None) {
04182             PyErr_SetString(PyExc_TypeError,
04183                 "instance exception may not have a separate value");
04184             goto raise_error;
04185         }
04186         /* Normalize to raise <class>, <instance> */
04187         Py_DECREF(value);
04188         value = type;
04189         #if PY_VERSION_HEX < 0x02050000
04190             if (PyInstance_Check(type)) {
04191                 type = (PyObject*) ((PyInstanceObject*)type)->in_class;
04192                 Py_INCREF(type);
04193             }
04194             else {
04195                 type = 0;
04196                 PyErr_SetString(PyExc_TypeError,
04197                     "raise: exception must be an old-style class or instance");
04198                 goto raise_error;
04199             }
04200         #else
04201             type = (PyObject*) Py_TYPE(type);
04202             Py_INCREF(type);
04203             if (!PyType_IsSubtype((PyTypeObject *)type, (PyTypeObject *)PyExc_BaseException)) {
04204                 PyErr_SetString(PyExc_TypeError,
04205                     "raise: exception class must be a subclass of BaseException");
04206                 goto raise_error;
04207             }
04208         #endif
04209     }
04210 
04211     __Pyx_ErrRestore(type, value, tb);
04212     return;
04213 raise_error:
04214     Py_XDECREF(value);
04215     Py_XDECREF(type);
04216     Py_XDECREF(tb);
04217     return;
04218 }
04219 
04220 #else /* Python 3+ */
04221 
04222 static void __Pyx_Raise(PyObject *type, PyObject *value, PyObject *tb, PyObject *cause) {
04223     if (tb == Py_None) {
04224         tb = 0;
04225     } else if (tb && !PyTraceBack_Check(tb)) {
04226         PyErr_SetString(PyExc_TypeError,
04227             "raise: arg 3 must be a traceback or None");
04228         goto bad;
04229     }
04230     if (value == Py_None)
04231         value = 0;
04232 
04233     if (PyExceptionInstance_Check(type)) {
04234         if (value) {
04235             PyErr_SetString(PyExc_TypeError,
04236                 "instance exception may not have a separate value");
04237             goto bad;
04238         }
04239         value = type;
04240         type = (PyObject*) Py_TYPE(value);
04241     } else if (!PyExceptionClass_Check(type)) {
04242         PyErr_SetString(PyExc_TypeError,
04243             "raise: exception class must be a subclass of BaseException");
04244         goto bad;
04245     }
04246 
04247     if (cause) {
04248         PyObject *fixed_cause;
04249         if (PyExceptionClass_Check(cause)) {
04250             fixed_cause = PyObject_CallObject(cause, NULL);
04251             if (fixed_cause == NULL)
04252                 goto bad;
04253         }
04254         else if (PyExceptionInstance_Check(cause)) {
04255             fixed_cause = cause;
04256             Py_INCREF(fixed_cause);
04257         }
04258         else {
04259             PyErr_SetString(PyExc_TypeError,
04260                             "exception causes must derive from "
04261                             "BaseException");
04262             goto bad;
04263         }
04264         if (!value) {
04265             value = PyObject_CallObject(type, NULL);
04266         }
04267         PyException_SetCause(value, fixed_cause);
04268     }
04269 
04270     PyErr_SetObject(type, value);
04271 
04272     if (tb) {
04273         PyThreadState *tstate = PyThreadState_GET();
04274         PyObject* tmp_tb = tstate->curexc_traceback;
04275         if (tb != tmp_tb) {
04276             Py_INCREF(tb);
04277             tstate->curexc_traceback = tb;
04278             Py_XDECREF(tmp_tb);
04279         }
04280     }
04281 
04282 bad:
04283     return;
04284 }
04285 #endif
04286 
04287 static CYTHON_INLINE void __Pyx_RaiseNeedMoreValuesError(Py_ssize_t index) {
04288     PyErr_Format(PyExc_ValueError,
04289                  "need more than %"PY_FORMAT_SIZE_T"d value%s to unpack",
04290                  index, (index == 1) ? "" : "s");
04291 }

04293 static CYTHON_INLINE void __Pyx_RaiseTooManyValuesError(Py_ssize_t expected) {
04294     PyErr_Format(PyExc_ValueError,
04295                  "too many values to unpack (expected %"PY_FORMAT_SIZE_T"d)", expected);
04296 }

04298 static CYTHON_INLINE void __Pyx_RaiseNoneNotIterableError(void) {
04299     PyErr_SetString(PyExc_TypeError, "'NoneType' object is not iterable");
04300 }
04301 
04302 static void __Pyx_UnpackTupleError(PyObject *t, Py_ssize_t index) {
04303     if (t == Py_None) {
04304       __Pyx_RaiseNoneNotIterableError();
04305     } else if (PyTuple_GET_SIZE(t) < index) {
04306       __Pyx_RaiseNeedMoreValuesError(PyTuple_GET_SIZE(t));
04307     } else {
04308       __Pyx_RaiseTooManyValuesError(index);
04309     }
04310 }

04312 static CYTHON_INLINE int __Pyx_TypeTest(PyObject *obj, PyTypeObject *type) {
04313     if (unlikely(!type)) {
04314         PyErr_Format(PyExc_SystemError, "Missing type object");
04315         return 0;
04316     }
04317     if (likely(PyObject_TypeCheck(obj, type)))
04318         return 1;
04319     PyErr_Format(PyExc_TypeError, "Cannot convert %.200s to %.200s",
04320                  Py_TYPE(obj)->tp_name, type->tp_name);
04321     return 0;
04322 }
04323 
04324 static PyObject *__Pyx_Import(PyObject *name, PyObject *from_list, long level) {
04325     PyObject *py_import = 0;
04326     PyObject *empty_list = 0;
04327     PyObject *module = 0;
04328     PyObject *global_dict = 0;
04329     PyObject *empty_dict = 0;
04330     PyObject *list;
04331     py_import = __Pyx_GetAttrString(__pyx_b, "__import__");
04332     if (!py_import)
04333         goto bad;
04334     if (from_list)
04335         list = from_list;
04336     else {
04337         empty_list = PyList_New(0);
04338         if (!empty_list)
04339             goto bad;
04340         list = empty_list;
04341     }
04342     global_dict = PyModule_GetDict(__pyx_m);
04343     if (!global_dict)
04344         goto bad;
04345     empty_dict = PyDict_New();
04346     if (!empty_dict)
04347         goto bad;
04348     #if PY_VERSION_HEX >= 0x02050000
04349     {
04350         PyObject *py_level = PyInt_FromLong(level);
04351         if (!py_level)
04352             goto bad;
04353         module = PyObject_CallFunctionObjArgs(py_import,
04354             name, global_dict, empty_dict, list, py_level, NULL);
04355         Py_DECREF(py_level);
04356     }
04357     #else
04358     if (level>0) {
04359         PyErr_SetString(PyExc_RuntimeError, "Relative import is not supported for Python <=2.4.");
04360         goto bad;
04361     }
04362     module = PyObject_CallFunctionObjArgs(py_import,
04363         name, global_dict, empty_dict, list, NULL);
04364     #endif
04365 bad:
04366     Py_XDECREF(empty_list);
04367     Py_XDECREF(py_import);
04368     Py_XDECREF(empty_dict);
04369     return module;
04370 }

04372 #if CYTHON_CCOMPLEX
04373   #ifdef __cplusplus
04374     static CYTHON_INLINE __pyx_t_float_complex __pyx_t_float_complex_from_parts(float x, float y) {
04375       return ::std::complex< float >(x, y);
04376     }
04377   #else
04378     static CYTHON_INLINE __pyx_t_float_complex __pyx_t_float_complex_from_parts(float x, float y) {
04379       return x + y*(__pyx_t_float_complex)_Complex_I;
04380     }
04381   #endif
04382 #else
04383     static CYTHON_INLINE __pyx_t_float_complex __pyx_t_float_complex_from_parts(float x, float y) {
04384       __pyx_t_float_complex z;
04385       z.real = x;
04386       z.imag = y;
04387       return z;
04388     }
04389 #endif
04390 
04391 #if CYTHON_CCOMPLEX
04392 #else
04393     static CYTHON_INLINE int __Pyx_c_eqf(__pyx_t_float_complex a, __pyx_t_float_complex b) {
04394        return (a.real == b.real) && (a.imag == b.imag);
04395     }
04396     static CYTHON_INLINE __pyx_t_float_complex __Pyx_c_sumf(__pyx_t_float_complex a, __pyx_t_float_complex b) {
04397         __pyx_t_float_complex z;
04398         z.real = a.real + b.real;
04399         z.imag = a.imag + b.imag;
04400         return z;
04401     }
04402     static CYTHON_INLINE __pyx_t_float_complex __Pyx_c_difff(__pyx_t_float_complex a, __pyx_t_float_complex b) {
04403         __pyx_t_float_complex z;
04404         z.real = a.real - b.real;
04405         z.imag = a.imag - b.imag;
04406         return z;
04407     }
04408     static CYTHON_INLINE __pyx_t_float_complex __Pyx_c_prodf(__pyx_t_float_complex a, __pyx_t_float_complex b) {
04409         __pyx_t_float_complex z;
04410         z.real = a.real * b.real - a.imag * b.imag;
04411         z.imag = a.real * b.imag + a.imag * b.real;
04412         return z;
04413     }
04414     static CYTHON_INLINE __pyx_t_float_complex __Pyx_c_quotf(__pyx_t_float_complex a, __pyx_t_float_complex b) {
04415         __pyx_t_float_complex z;
04416         float denom = b.real * b.real + b.imag * b.imag;
04417         z.real = (a.real * b.real + a.imag * b.imag) / denom;
04418         z.imag = (a.imag * b.real - a.real * b.imag) / denom;
04419         return z;
04420     }
04421     static CYTHON_INLINE __pyx_t_float_complex __Pyx_c_negf(__pyx_t_float_complex a) {
04422         __pyx_t_float_complex z;
04423         z.real = -a.real;
04424         z.imag = -a.imag;
04425         return z;
04426     }
04427     static CYTHON_INLINE int __Pyx_c_is_zerof(__pyx_t_float_complex a) {
04428        return (a.real == 0) && (a.imag == 0);
04429     }
04430     static CYTHON_INLINE __pyx_t_float_complex __Pyx_c_conjf(__pyx_t_float_complex a) {
04431         __pyx_t_float_complex z;
04432         z.real =  a.real;
04433         z.imag = -a.imag;
04434         return z;
04435     }
04436     #if 1
04437         static CYTHON_INLINE float __Pyx_c_absf(__pyx_t_float_complex z) {
04438           #if !defined(HAVE_HYPOT) || defined(_MSC_VER)
04439             return sqrtf(z.real*z.real + z.imag*z.imag);
04440           #else
04441             return hypotf(z.real, z.imag);
04442           #endif
04443         }
04444         static CYTHON_INLINE __pyx_t_float_complex __Pyx_c_powf(__pyx_t_float_complex a, __pyx_t_float_complex b) {
04445             __pyx_t_float_complex z;
04446             float r, lnr, theta, z_r, z_theta;
04447             if (b.imag == 0 && b.real == (int)b.real) {
04448                 if (b.real < 0) {
04449                     float denom = a.real * a.real + a.imag * a.imag;
04450                     a.real = a.real / denom;
04451                     a.imag = -a.imag / denom;
04452                     b.real = -b.real;
04453                 }
04454                 switch ((int)b.real) {
04455                     case 0:
04456                         z.real = 1;
04457                         z.imag = 0;
04458                         return z;
04459                     case 1:
04460                         return a;
04461                     case 2:
04462                         z = __Pyx_c_prodf(a, a);
04463                         return __Pyx_c_prodf(a, a);
04464                     case 3:
04465                         z = __Pyx_c_prodf(a, a);
04466                         return __Pyx_c_prodf(z, a);
04467                     case 4:
04468                         z = __Pyx_c_prodf(a, a);
04469                         return __Pyx_c_prodf(z, z);
04470                 }
04471             }
04472             if (a.imag == 0) {
04473                 if (a.real == 0) {
04474                     return a;
04475                 }
04476                 r = a.real;
04477                 theta = 0;
04478             } else {
04479                 r = __Pyx_c_absf(a);
04480                 theta = atan2f(a.imag, a.real);
04481             }
04482             lnr = logf(r);
04483             z_r = expf(lnr * b.real - theta * b.imag);
04484             z_theta = theta * b.real + lnr * b.imag;
04485             z.real = z_r * cosf(z_theta);
04486             z.imag = z_r * sinf(z_theta);
04487             return z;
04488         }
04489     #endif
04490 #endif

04493   #ifdef __cplusplus

04500     }

04511 #if CYTHON_CCOMPLEX
04512 #else
04513     static CYTHON_INLINE int __Pyx_c_eq(__pyx_t_double_complex a, __pyx_t_double_complex b) {
04514        return (a.real == b.real) && (a.imag == b.imag);
04515     }
04516     static CYTHON_INLINE __pyx_t_double_complex __Pyx_c_sum(__pyx_t_double_complex a, __pyx_t_double_complex b) {
04517         __pyx_t_double_complex z;
04518         z.real = a.real + b.real;
04519         z.imag = a.imag + b.imag;
04520         return z;
04521     }
04522     static CYTHON_INLINE __pyx_t_double_complex __Pyx_c_diff(__pyx_t_double_complex a, __pyx_t_double_complex b) {
04523         __pyx_t_double_complex z;
04524         z.real = a.real - b.real;
04525         z.imag = a.imag - b.imag;
04526         return z;
04527     }
04528     static CYTHON_INLINE __pyx_t_double_complex __Pyx_c_prod(__pyx_t_double_complex a, __pyx_t_double_complex b) {
04529         __pyx_t_double_complex z;
04530         z.real = a.real * b.real - a.imag * b.imag;
04531         z.imag = a.real * b.imag + a.imag * b.real;
04532         return z;
04533     }
04534     static CYTHON_INLINE __pyx_t_double_complex __Pyx_c_quot(__pyx_t_double_complex a, __pyx_t_double_complex b) {
04535         __pyx_t_double_complex z;
04536         double denom = b.real * b.real + b.imag * b.imag;
04537         z.real = (a.real * b.real + a.imag * b.imag) / denom;
04538         z.imag = (a.imag * b.real - a.real * b.imag) / denom;
04539         return z;
04540     }
04541     static CYTHON_INLINE __pyx_t_double_complex __Pyx_c_neg(__pyx_t_double_complex a) {
04542         __pyx_t_double_complex z;
04543         z.real = -a.real;
04544         z.imag = -a.imag;
04545         return z;
04546     }
04547     static CYTHON_INLINE int __Pyx_c_is_zero(__pyx_t_double_complex a) {
04548        return (a.real == 0) && (a.imag == 0);
04549     }
04550     static CYTHON_INLINE __pyx_t_double_complex __Pyx_c_conj(__pyx_t_double_complex a) {
04551         __pyx_t_double_complex z;
04552         z.real =  a.real;
04553         z.imag = -a.imag;
04554         return z;
04555     }
04556     #if 1
04557         static CYTHON_INLINE double __Pyx_c_abs(__pyx_t_double_complex z) {
04558           #if !defined(HAVE_HYPOT) || defined(_MSC_VER)
04559             return sqrt(z.real*z.real + z.imag*z.imag);
04560           #else
04561             return hypot(z.real, z.imag);
04562           #endif
04563         }
04564         static CYTHON_INLINE __pyx_t_double_complex __Pyx_c_pow(__pyx_t_double_complex a, __pyx_t_double_complex b) {
04565             __pyx_t_double_complex z;
04566             double r, lnr, theta, z_r, z_theta;
04567             if (b.imag == 0 && b.real == (int)b.real) {
04568                 if (b.real < 0) {
04569                     double denom = a.real * a.real + a.imag * a.imag;
04570                     a.real = a.real / denom;
04571                     a.imag = -a.imag / denom;
04572                     b.real = -b.real;
04573                 }
04574                 switch ((int)b.real) {
04575                     case 0:
04576                         z.real = 1;
04577                         z.imag = 0;
04578                         return z;
04579                     case 1:
04580                         return a;
04581                     case 2:
04582                         z = __Pyx_c_prod(a, a);
04583                         return __Pyx_c_prod(a, a);
04584                     case 3:
04585                         z = __Pyx_c_prod(a, a);
04586                         return __Pyx_c_prod(z, a);
04587                     case 4:
04588                         z = __Pyx_c_prod(a, a);
04589                         return __Pyx_c_prod(z, z);
04590                 }
04591             }
04592             if (a.imag == 0) {
04593                 if (a.real == 0) {
04594                     return a;
04595                 }
04596                 r = a.real;
04597                 theta = 0;
04598             } else {
04599                 r = __Pyx_c_abs(a);
04600                 theta = atan2(a.imag, a.real);
04601             }
04602             lnr = log(r);
04603             z_r = exp(lnr * b.real - theta * b.imag);
04604             z_theta = theta * b.real + lnr * b.imag;
04605             z.real = z_r * cos(z_theta);
04606             z.imag = z_r * sin(z_theta);
04607             return z;
04608         }
04609     #endif
04610 #endif

04996                 return (signed PY_LONG_LONG)-1;
04997             }
04998             return (signed PY_LONG_LONG)PyLong_AsUnsignedLongLong(x);
04999         } else {
05000             return (signed PY_LONG_LONG)PyLong_AsLongLong(x);
05001         }
05002     } else {
05003         signed PY_LONG_LONG val;
05004         PyObject *tmp = __Pyx_PyNumber_Int(x);
05005         if (!tmp) return (signed PY_LONG_LONG)-1;
05006         val = __Pyx_PyInt_AsSignedLongLong(tmp);
05007         Py_DECREF(tmp);
05008         return val;
05009     }
05010 }
05011 
05012 static int __Pyx_check_binary_version(void) {
05013     char ctversion[4], rtversion[4];
05014     PyOS_snprintf(ctversion, 4, "%d.%d", PY_MAJOR_VERSION, PY_MINOR_VERSION);
05015     PyOS_snprintf(rtversion, 4, "%s", Py_GetVersion());
05016     if (ctversion[0] != rtversion[0] || ctversion[2] != rtversion[2]) {
05017         char message[200];
05018         PyOS_snprintf(message, sizeof(message),
05019                       "compiletime version %s of module '%.100s' "
05020                       "does not match runtime version %s",
05021                       ctversion, __Pyx_MODULE_NAME, rtversion);
05022         #if PY_VERSION_HEX < 0x02050000
05023         return PyErr_Warn(NULL, message);
05024         #else
05025         return PyErr_WarnEx(NULL, message, 1);
05026         #endif
05027     }
05028     return 0;
05029 }

05031 static int __Pyx_SetVtable(PyObject *dict, void *vtable) {
05032 #if PY_VERSION_HEX >= 0x02070000 && !(PY_MAJOR_VERSION==3&&PY_MINOR_VERSION==0)
05033     PyObject *ob = PyCapsule_New(vtable, 0, 0);
05034 #else
05035     PyObject *ob = PyCObject_FromVoidPtr(vtable, 0);
05036 #endif
05037     if (!ob)
05038         goto bad;
05039     if (PyDict_SetItemString(dict, "__pyx_vtable__", ob) < 0)
05040         goto bad;
05041     Py_DECREF(ob);
05042     return 0;
05043 bad:
05044     Py_XDECREF(ob);
05045     return -1;
05046 }

05048 #ifndef __PYX_HAVE_RT_ImportType
05049 #define __PYX_HAVE_RT_ImportType
05050 static PyTypeObject *__Pyx_ImportType(const char *module_name, const char *class_name,
05051     size_t size, int strict)
05052 {
05053     PyObject *py_module = 0;
05054     PyObject *result = 0;
05055     PyObject *py_name = 0;
05056     char warning[200];
05057 
05058     py_module = __Pyx_ImportModule(module_name);
05059     if (!py_module)
05060         goto bad;
05061     #if PY_MAJOR_VERSION < 3
05062     py_name = PyString_FromString(class_name);
05063     #else
05064     py_name = PyUnicode_FromString(class_name);
05065     #endif
05066     if (!py_name)
05067         goto bad;
05068     result = PyObject_GetAttr(py_module, py_name);
05069     Py_DECREF(py_name);
05070     py_name = 0;
05071     Py_DECREF(py_module);
05072     py_module = 0;
05073     if (!result)
05074         goto bad;
05075     if (!PyType_Check(result)) {
05076         PyErr_Format(PyExc_TypeError,
05077             "%s.%s is not a type object",
05078             module_name, class_name);
05079         goto bad;
05080     }
05081     if (!strict && ((PyTypeObject *)result)->tp_basicsize > (Py_ssize_t)size) {
05082         PyOS_snprintf(warning, sizeof(warning),
05083             "%s.%s size changed, may indicate binary incompatibility",
05084             module_name, class_name);
05085         #if PY_VERSION_HEX < 0x02050000
05086         if (PyErr_Warn(NULL, warning) < 0) goto bad;
05087         #else
05088         if (PyErr_WarnEx(NULL, warning, 0) < 0) goto bad;
05089         #endif
05090     }
05091     else if (((PyTypeObject *)result)->tp_basicsize != (Py_ssize_t)size) {
05092         PyErr_Format(PyExc_ValueError,
05093             "%s.%s has the wrong size, try recompiling",
05094             module_name, class_name);
05095         goto bad;
05096     }
05097     return (PyTypeObject *)result;
05098 bad:
05099     Py_XDECREF(py_module);
05100     Py_XDECREF(result);
05101     return NULL;
05102 }
05103 #endif
05104 
05105 #ifndef __PYX_HAVE_RT_ImportModule
05106 #define __PYX_HAVE_RT_ImportModule
05107 static PyObject *__Pyx_ImportModule(const char *name) {
05108     PyObject *py_name = 0;
05109     PyObject *py_module = 0;
05110 
05111     #if PY_MAJOR_VERSION < 3
05112     py_name = PyString_FromString(name);
05113     #else
05114     py_name = PyUnicode_FromString(name);
05115     #endif
05116     if (!py_name)
05117         goto bad;
05118     py_module = PyImport_Import(py_name);
05119     Py_DECREF(py_name);
05120     return py_module;
05121 bad:
05122     Py_XDECREF(py_name);
05123     return 0;
05124 }
05125 #endif

05127 #include "compile.h"

05130 
05131 static void __Pyx_AddTraceback(const char *funcname, int __pyx_clineno,
05132                                int __pyx_lineno, const char *__pyx_filename) {
05133     PyObject *py_srcfile = 0;
05134     PyObject *py_funcname = 0;
05135     PyObject *py_globals = 0;
05136     PyCodeObject *py_code = 0;
05137     PyFrameObject *py_frame = 0;
05138 
05139     #if PY_MAJOR_VERSION < 3
05140     py_srcfile = PyString_FromString(__pyx_filename);
05141     #else
05142     py_srcfile = PyUnicode_FromString(__pyx_filename);
05143     #endif
05144     if (!py_srcfile) goto bad;
05145     if (__pyx_clineno) {
05146         #if PY_MAJOR_VERSION < 3
05147         py_funcname = PyString_FromFormat( "%s (%s:%d)", funcname, __pyx_cfilenm, __pyx_clineno);
05148         #else
05149         py_funcname = PyUnicode_FromFormat( "%s (%s:%d)", funcname, __pyx_cfilenm, __pyx_clineno);
05150         #endif
05151     }
05152     else {
05153         #if PY_MAJOR_VERSION < 3
05154         py_funcname = PyString_FromString(funcname);
05155         #else
05156         py_funcname = PyUnicode_FromString(funcname);
05157         #endif
05158     }
05159     if (!py_funcname) goto bad;
05160     py_globals = PyModule_GetDict(__pyx_m);
05161     if (!py_globals) goto bad;
05162     py_code = PyCode_New(
05163         0,            /*int argcount,*/
05164         #if PY_MAJOR_VERSION >= 3
05165         0,            /*int kwonlyargcount,*/
05166         #endif
05167         0,            /*int nlocals,*/
05168         0,            /*int stacksize,*/
05169         0,            /*int flags,*/
05170         __pyx_empty_bytes, /*PyObject *code,*/
05171         __pyx_empty_tuple,  /*PyObject *consts,*/
05172         __pyx_empty_tuple,  /*PyObject *names,*/
05173         __pyx_empty_tuple,  /*PyObject *varnames,*/
05174         __pyx_empty_tuple,  /*PyObject *freevars,*/
05175         __pyx_empty_tuple,  /*PyObject *cellvars,*/
05176         py_srcfile,   /*PyObject *filename,*/
05177         py_funcname,  /*PyObject *name,*/
05178         __pyx_lineno,   /*int firstlineno,*/
05179         __pyx_empty_bytes  /*PyObject *lnotab*/
05180     );
05181     if (!py_code) goto bad;
05182     py_frame = PyFrame_New(
05183         PyThreadState_GET(), /*PyThreadState *tstate,*/
05184         py_code,             /*PyCodeObject *code,*/
05185         py_globals,          /*PyObject *globals,*/
05186         0                    /*PyObject *locals*/
05187     );
05188     if (!py_frame) goto bad;
05189     py_frame->f_lineno = __pyx_lineno;
05190     PyTraceBack_Here(py_frame);
05191 bad:
05192     Py_XDECREF(py_srcfile);
05193     Py_XDECREF(py_funcname);
05194     Py_XDECREF(py_code);
05195     Py_XDECREF(py_frame);
05196 }

05198 static int __Pyx_InitStrings(__Pyx_StringTabEntry *t) {
05199     while (t->p) {
05200         #if PY_MAJOR_VERSION < 3
05201         if (t->is_unicode) {
05202             *t->p = PyUnicode_DecodeUTF8(t->s, t->n - 1, NULL);
05203         } else if (t->intern) {
05204             *t->p = PyString_InternFromString(t->s);
05205         } else {
05206             *t->p = PyString_FromStringAndSize(t->s, t->n - 1);
05207         }
05208         #else  /* Python 3+ has unicode identifiers */
05209         if (t->is_unicode | t->is_str) {
05210             if (t->intern) {
05211                 *t->p = PyUnicode_InternFromString(t->s);
05212             } else if (t->encoding) {
05213                 *t->p = PyUnicode_Decode(t->s, t->n - 1, t->encoding, NULL);
05214             } else {
05215                 *t->p = PyUnicode_FromStringAndSize(t->s, t->n - 1);
05216             }
05217         } else {
05218             *t->p = PyBytes_FromStringAndSize(t->s, t->n - 1);
05219         }
05220         #endif
05221         if (!*t->p)
05222             return -1;
05223         ++t;
05224     }
05225     return 0;
05226 }

05230 static CYTHON_INLINE int __Pyx_PyObject_IsTrue(PyObject* x) {
05231    int is_true = x == Py_True;
05232    if (is_true | (x == Py_False) | (x == Py_None)) return is_true;
05233    else return PyObject_IsTrue(x);
05234 }
05235 
05236 static CYTHON_INLINE PyObject* __Pyx_PyNumber_Int(PyObject* x) {
05237   PyNumberMethods *m;
05238   const char *name = NULL;
05239   PyObject *res = NULL;
05240 #if PY_VERSION_HEX < 0x03000000
05241   if (PyInt_Check(x) || PyLong_Check(x))
05242 #else
05243   if (PyLong_Check(x))
05244 #endif
05245     return Py_INCREF(x), x;
05246   m = Py_TYPE(x)->tp_as_number;
05247 #if PY_VERSION_HEX < 0x03000000
05248   if (m && m->nb_int) {
05249     name = "int";
05250     res = PyNumber_Int(x);
05251   }
05252   else if (m && m->nb_long) {
05253     name = "long";
05254     res = PyNumber_Long(x);
05255   }
05256 #else
05257   if (m && m->nb_int) {
05258     name = "int";
05259     res = PyNumber_Long(x);
05260   }
05261 #endif
05262   if (res) {
05263 #if PY_VERSION_HEX < 0x03000000
05264     if (!PyInt_Check(res) && !PyLong_Check(res)) {
05265 #else
05266     if (!PyLong_Check(res)) {
05267 #endif
05268       PyErr_Format(PyExc_TypeError,
05269                    "__%s__ returned non-%s (type %.200s)",
05270                    name, name, Py_TYPE(res)->tp_name);
05271       Py_DECREF(res);
05272       return NULL;
05273     }
05274   }
05275   else if (!PyErr_Occurred()) {
05276     PyErr_SetString(PyExc_TypeError,
05277                     "an integer is required");
05278   }
05279   return res;
05280 }
05281 
05282 static CYTHON_INLINE Py_ssize_t __Pyx_PyIndex_AsSsize_t(PyObject* b) {
05283   Py_ssize_t ival;
05284   PyObject* x = PyNumber_Index(b);
05285   if (!x) return -1;
05286   ival = PyInt_AsSsize_t(x);
05287   Py_DECREF(x);
05288   return ival;
05289 }
05290 
05291 static CYTHON_INLINE PyObject * __Pyx_PyInt_FromSize_t(size_t ival) {
05292 #if PY_VERSION_HEX < 0x02050000
05293    if (ival <= LONG_MAX)
05294        return PyInt_FromLong((long)ival);
05295    else {
05296        unsigned char *bytes = (unsigned char *) &ival;
05297        int one = 1; int little = (int)*(unsigned char*)&one;
05298        return _PyLong_FromByteArray(bytes, sizeof(size_t), little, 0);
05299    }
05300 #else
05301    return PyInt_FromSize_t(ival);
05302 #endif
05303 }
05304 
05305 static CYTHON_INLINE size_t __Pyx_PyInt_AsSize_t(PyObject* x) {
05306    unsigned PY_LONG_LONG val = __Pyx_PyInt_AsUnsignedLongLong(x);
05307    if (unlikely(val == (unsigned PY_LONG_LONG)-1 && PyErr_Occurred())) {
05308        return (size_t)-1;
05309    } else if (unlikely(val != (unsigned PY_LONG_LONG)(size_t)val)) {
05310        PyErr_SetString(PyExc_OverflowError,
05311                        "value too large to convert to size_t");
05312        return (size_t)-1;
05313    }
05314    return (size_t)val;
05315 }
